<DIV style="position:absolute;top:584;left:528"><font style="font-
size:6.8pt;line-height:10px;">Harmony Gold Mining Company Limited <br>(Harmony),
a world-class gold mining and <br>exploration company, has operations and 
<br>assets in South Africa and Papua New <br>Guinea. Harmony, which has more 
than 60 <br>years&#8217; experience in the industry, is the third <br>largest 
gold producer in South Africa. Our <br>assets include 9 underground mines and 1 
<br>open pit operation and several surface <br>sources in South Africa. Our 
assets in PNG &#8211;<br>an open pit mine (Hidden Valley), as well as <br>the 
significant Golpu project &#8211; are held in a <br>joint venture. We also own 
several <br>exploration tenements, in Papua New <br>Guinea. </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:748;left:528"><font style="font-
size:6.8pt;line-height:10px;">The company&#8217;s primary stock exchange 
<br>listing is on the JSE with a secondary listing <br>on the New York Stock 
Exchange. The bulk <br>of our shareholders are in South Africa and <br>the 
United States. Additional information on <br>the company is available on the 
corporate <br>website, </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:810;left:563"><font style="font-
size:6.8pt;color:#2964af;">www.harmony.co.za</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:810;left:644"><font style="font-
size:6.8pt;">.</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:818;left:528"><font style="font-size:11.9pt;">
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:844;left:528"><font style="font-size:11.9pt;">
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:221;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;"><b>TRADING STATEMENT FOR THE YEAR ENDED 30 JUNE 2016 
</b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:251;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;"><b>Johannesburg.  12 August 2016</b>: In terms of 
paragraph 3.4(b) of the Listings <br>Requirements of the JSE Limited, a company 
listed on the JSE is required to <br>publish a trading statement as soon as they
are satisfied that a reasonable <br>degree of certainty exists that the 
financial results for the period to be reported <br>upon next will differ by at 
least 20% from the financial results for the previous <br>corresponding 
period.</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:354;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">Shareholders of Harmony Gold Mining Company 
Limited (&#8220;Harmony&#8221; and/or &#8220;the <br>Company&#8221;) are advised
that a reasonable degree of certainty exist that earnings <br>for the year ended
30 June 2016 will be higher than for the year ended 30 June <br>2015 (&#8220;the
previous comparable period&#8221;), primarily due to a 21% increase in the 
<br>average rand gold price.</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:442;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">Headline earnings per share (&#8220;HEPS&#8221;)
are expected to be between 202 and 240 <br>SA cents per share, which is between 
207% and 227% (or between 391 and 429 <br>SA cents per share) higher than the 
headline loss of 189 SA cents per share <br>reported for the previous comparable
period in 2015. </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:515;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">In US dollars terms, HEPS are expected to be 
between 13 and 16 US cents per <br>share, which is between 180% and 200% (or 
between 29 and 32 US cents per <br>share) higher than the headline loss of 16 US
cents per share reported for the <br>previous comparable period in 2015. 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:589;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">Earnings per share (&#8220;EPS&#8221;) are 
expected to be between 200 and 238 SA cents <br>per share, which is between 119%
and 123% (or between 1 244 and 1 282 cents <br>per share) higher than the loss 
of 1 044 SA cents per share reported for the <br>previous comparable period. 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:662;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">In US dollar terms, EPS are expected to be between
13 and 16 US cents per <br>share, which is between 115% and 119% (or between 99 
and 102 US cents per <br>share) higher than the loss of 86 US cents per share 
reported for the previous <br>comparable period. </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:735;left:58"><font style="font-
size:9.2pt;line-height:17px;">The financial information on which this trading 
statement has been based, has <br>not been reviewed or reported on by 
Harmony&#8217;s external auditors. Harmony will <br>publish its financial 
results for the year ended 30 June 2016 on 17 August 2016.  <br>Please refer to 
our website for the details of the results event 
<br>www.harmony.co.za.</font></DIV>
